\doxysection{TMPro.\+TMP\+\_\+\+Text Class Reference}

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Base class which contains common properties and functions shared between the Text\+Mesh\+Pro and Text\+Mesh\+Pro\+UGUI component.

\index{TMPro.TMP\_Text@{TMPro.TMP\_Text}!vertexBufferAutoSizeReduction@{vertexBufferAutoSizeReduction}}
\index{vertexBufferAutoSizeReduction@{vertexBufferAutoSizeReduction}!TMPro.TMP\_Text@{TMPro.TMP\_Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vertexBufferAutoSizeReduction}{vertexBufferAutoSizeReduction}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool TMPro.\+TMP\+\_\+\+Text.\+vertex\+Buffer\+Auto\+Size\+Reduction\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [get]}, {\ttfamily [set]}}



Determines if the data structures allocated to contain the geometry of the text object will be reduced in size if the number of characters required to display the text is reduced by more than 256 characters. This reduction has the benefit of reducing the amount of vertex data being submitted to the graphic device but results in GC when it occurs.
